msg:This time my family traveled by car and passed through more than ten cities before staying in Tengchong for one more night in a villa hot spring courtyard. I didn't expect to encounter such a stunning hotel. This hotel is also the only one that made us feel nostalgic and still stay. I have the urge to stay again, and I can evaluate the hotel in several aspects. 1. The hotel is a garden-like structure, built on the mountain. The room we stayed in is the highest. The entire yard is carefully built with a water system, which is very delicate. 2. The hotel is not in the ancient city, but 700 meters away from the ancient city. Fortunately, I did not live in the ancient city. The battery car sent there not only gave me a different experience, but also allowed me to stroll through the streets of the county and feel the real rhythm of life of the local people. 3. Our family has relatively high requirements for accommodation. We have basically stayed in some of the better five-star and platinum hotels in China. Most of them have no service features. The service attitude of this hotel is the best and most proactive I have ever seen. It shows. The boss has a strong sense of service and the employees are all locals, which also shows that the people in Phoenix in western Hunan are very simple and kind-hearted. 4. You can order food in the hotel restaurant, and you will be notified when the meal is ready. You can sit down and eat in the restaurant. I prefer heavy food, and I also like to eat Hunan cuisine. The food tastes very authentic. A few suggestions: Separate dry and wet areas in the toilet, install an automatic sensor on the curtain, and replace the door lock with a card swipe system to make it more convenient. Many friends want to experience it after seeing my lover‚Äôs post on Moments. Finally, I wish everyone at Phoenix Snow Qingji a happy new year.

The name of the B&B is Xueqing, which comes from the title of Shen Congwen's collection of essays published by Jiangsu Publishing House. Following Shen Congwen's thoughts while traveling through the ancient city is quite creative. The courtyard decoration is full of the charm of Jiangnan courtyard, with pavilions, waterside pavilions and winding paths. In particular, there is a reading space that stores literature and books related to Shen Congwen and Huang Yongyu, which is very helpful for a deep understanding of Phoenix... 3. Warm service and good facilities. There are battery cars that shuttle between scenic spots and B&Bs at any time. The bathrooms are equipped with laundry detergent and disinfectant. msg:This is the first time to write a comment on the platform, dedicated to Xueqingji, which is perfect and has no dead ends:
This time I came to Fenghuang, because I stayed at Xueqingji, the whole trip became especially beautiful.
Once in the hotel, from the security guy at the door to the front desk, everyone is very kind, not the indifference of a five-star hotel, nor the fake enthusiasm purely to attract business, but just right and amiable. The housekeeper, Xiao Teng, saw that we had brought two children, and immediately gave us double gifts of snacks and upgraded our room. (In addition, the hotel provided us with four sets of toothbrush sets and towels every day.) Seeing us coming back from the outside at night, he also kindly asked if we would go back to the room immediately, and brought us hot good night milk.
The whole hotel has winding paths leading to secluded places, winding water and stacking springs. It has the beauty of Jiangnan gardens. Various garden sketches, water lilies, hydrangeas, five-color plums, etc. are in full bloom at will. There is also the interest of the mountains and the wild. If you are not careful, you will encounter a red-billed blue jay pacing demurely. Strolling around the hotel can also kill half a day.
The most surprising thing about the B&B is the two theme halls, one of which houses various Shen Congwen-themed (also Huang Yongyu, Wang Zengqi, etc.) books, letters, etc. Another collection includes ancient books, rubbings, and rubbings, including Guqin, Go and other literati games. The interior decoration is elegant and breathtaking.
What children like most is the constant temperature swimming pool in the park. The real-time display shows that the water temperature is kept at about 35 degrees.
It is recommended that everyone who comes to Fenghuang stay at Xueqingji, which will definitely enhance the happiness of travel!

Talk about bad things, make me angry, let me score a point. The hotel is outside the ancient city, and you can call a battery car to pick you up every day. Every time the pick-up and drop-off location is fixed (I stayed for two nights and went to the ancient city no less than 5 times), something unbearable happened to me when I called the car back to the hotel on the second night. My group of 3 and 4 other guests were waiting for the battery car to arrive at the pick-up point. The 4 guests may have been waiting for a long time and became impatient. They chose to wait while walking back, and we chose to continue waiting at the pick-up point. However, after the 4 residents walked for 20 meters, they met the battery car and got on the car. I thought the battery car would continue to come down, because when I communicated with the front desk, I said that there were two groups of guests. Who knew the battery car After picking up the 4 residents, he turned around and walked away... While he was walking, I was still yelling at the back. The 4 residents heard me yelling, but the security didn't seem to hear it? Let's go straight away, here is a situation, this battery car can definitely sit the two groups of us, and it is not crowded. I immediately called the front desk to ask what was going on. The front desk said that they had informed the security guard that there were two groups of guests. Maybe the security guard was confused and needed to call to find out the situation. If it‚Äôs just like this, it‚Äôs okay. What makes me most angry is that when the security guard sent the 4 guests and came back to pick us up with an empty car, he didn‚Äôt drive to the pick-up point where we were, but left after seeing us. After 20 meters, we started to make a U-turn, and then parked on the opposite side of the road, waiting for us to walk over! *****, I'm not delicate, it's not that I don't want to walk the 20 meters, but the deliberate behavior of this security guard made me feel disrespected. Why should he vent his emotions on our guests? What's more, it was the security guard who was wrong. He should have been reprimanded by the front desk for not receiving me at first, so he used this method to vent his emotions. After responding to the hotel, I found that this is not the first time that this security guard has been complained about. If this kind of service awareness can still stay in your hotel, it can only show that the security guard is very hard-working and is a relative of the boss. It's been a long time since I encountered such a bad thing. I hope the hotel can handle this security guard well, and don't let the efforts of other people in the hotel go to waste because of him!
